			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Like other companies,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> we are in a challenging inflationary environment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> which has continued to deteriorate our gross margin</font><a name="_Hlk91153050"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">We are focused and committed to managing our business </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">so that we can restore gross margin to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> or above</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> our target of 55 percent over the long</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">er</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">-term. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">We will restore our gross margin over the near-term by implementing price increases to offset the higher input costs we are experiencing. Over the longer-term our margin accretive Must-Win Battles will further enhance gross margin.&#x201D; </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">As we look to the remainder of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">fiscal year, we&#x2019;ve</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> reduced our net income</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> guidance </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">by approximately two percent </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">for the full fiscal year </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the challenging inflationary environment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> we are </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">currently </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">operating in.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> However, we have been able to maintain our </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">revenue guidance</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">believe</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> we will finish fiscal year</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> 2022</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> with </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">both</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> topline</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and bottom-line</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> growth</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,&#x201D; Ridge concluded.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">greater</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> product availability</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> as a result of</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">adjustments </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the Company</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> made </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> its</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> United States </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">supply chain to increase the production capacity of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">its</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">highest volume </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">products</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. In addition, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">price increases that </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">took</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> effect in the first quarter of this fiscal year</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">contributed to increased sales in the</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">United States</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> from period to period</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> Net</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ales in </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Latin America increased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in the second quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. This growth was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">driven by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">successful promotional programs</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">increased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">product availability</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the favorable impact of</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> price increases,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the timing of customer orders</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ales in Canada</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">declined</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> 2 percent in the second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">quarter.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font></p></td></tr></table></div>

		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">Net sales of maintenance products, which are considered the primary growth focus for the Company, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">increased</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">19 percent</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> in </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">second quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;"> when compared to the prior year fiscal </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">This </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">increase </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">was primarily attributable to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">creased sales of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> Multi-Use Product </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">and WD-40 Specialist</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> all three segments</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">driven </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the favorable impact of price increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales of homecare and cleaning products </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">de</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">creased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">12</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">second quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> when compared to the prior year fiscal quarter. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> homecare and cleaning products, particularly </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">those </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in the U</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">nited States</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, are considered harvest brands providing healthy profits to the Company and are becoming a smaller part of the business as net sales of maintenance products grow</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, reflecting</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the execution of the Company&#x2019;s strategic initiatives.&nbsp; </font></p></td></tr></table></div>

Under the plan the Company is authorized to acquire up to $75.0 million of its outstanding shares through August 31, 2023. The timing and amount of repurchases will be based on terms and conditions acceptable to the Company and in compliance with applicable laws and regulations. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">During the period from November 1, 2021 through February 28, 2022, the Company repurchased 78,637 shares of its common stock at a total cost of $18.2 million, leaving $56.8 million available for the repurchase of common stock under this plan.</font>

		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About WD-40 Company</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Company is a global marketing organization dedicated to creating positive lasting memories by developing and selling products that solve problems in workshops, factories and homes around the world. The Company owns a wide range of well-known brands that include maintenance products and homecare and cleaning products: WD-40</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> Multi-Use Product, WD-40 Specialist</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 3-IN-ONE</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, GT85</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 2000 Flushes</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, no vac</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 1001</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, Spot Shot</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, Lava&#xAE;, Solvol</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, X-14</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, and Carpet Fresh</font><sub style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xAE;</sub><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Headquartered in San Diego, WD-40 Company recorded net sales of $488.1 million in fiscal year 2021 and its products are currently available in more than </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">176</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> countries and territories worldwide. WD-40 Company is traded on the NASDAQ Global Select market under the ticker symbol &#x201C;WDFC.&#x201D; For additional information about WD-40 Company please visit http://www.wd40company.com.</font>
		</p>
